4--7 and 8--11&200&\mbox{RK}\\
}
\renewcommand{\Gcb}{\Gcc{\item Either stations and 3 or stations 4 to 11 can be used.

\item Stations 1 and 3 can each carry a 100 gal (450L) FT.

\item Ventral station 2 can only be used to carry a jettisonable conformal 175 gal (800L) FT with a weight of 1,600, 3.0/2.0 load points, and 70 fuel points. While carried, the FT restricts the maximum speed to 4.0.

\item Stations 4 to 11 can each carry two RP-3 RK.

}}
\renewcommand{\Gda}{6/4/2/1}

\item Low roll rate (LRR). 

\item Flight Restrictions. UD, VD, ZC, and VC are forbidden. SC and SD may only use 1 VFP per turn. SD may only lose 1 altitude level per VFP.

\item Gun Turrets. Equipped with ten 23 mm NS-23 cannons in turrets and in the tail. They can fire in any direction. They may return fire twice per game turn in response to a gun attacks or conduct a single attack. The roll to hit is 2/1/1 and the AtA rating is 4. Gun attacks are modified only by the target size and have a $-1$ modifier when firing into the $60-$ arc. Ammunition is unlimited.

Each can carry up to (a) two 4,000 lb bombs, (b) four 2,000 lb bombs, (c) six 1,000 lb bombs, (d) twenty 500 lb bombs, or (e) two 640 gal FTs (each 2400L, weight 4,000, and 200 fuel points). All bombs must be the same type and low-drag.

\item As an exception to the normal rules for load points, internal loads contribute 1 load point for each 1,000 of weight and internal fuel contributes 1 load point for each 50 fuel points. A return mission will typically require leaving the target with at least 750 fuel points (15 load points).

}}

\renewcommand{\Fu}{\Fua{\item  Medium bomber version. NATO reporting name is Beagle.

\item High transonic drag (HTD). 

\item Low roll rate (LRR). 

\item Bomb system is ballistic ($-1$) if doing level bombing from four or more altitude levels above the target.

\item Tail Guns. In addition to its fixed guns, there aircraft has a tail mount with two 23 mm NR-23 guns. It can fire into the $60-$ arc. It may return fire twice per game turn in response to a gun attacks or conduct a single attack. Roll to hit is 3/2/1 and no modifiers apply except target size. The AtA rating is 4. The ammunition is 6.0.

\item Tail gunner has no ejection seat and can only bail out.

\item RWR from 1960.

\item \href{\detokenize{https://bit.ly/4fQBN9Q}}{ADC page on GitHub}.

}}

2&4,400&\mbox{BB}\\
}

\renewcommand{\Fu}{\Fua{\item  Nuclear strike version. NATO reporting name is Beagle.

\item High transonic drag (HTD). 

\item Low roll rate (LRR). 

\item Bomb system is ballistic ($-1$) if doing level bombing from four or more altitude levels above the target.

\item Tail Guns. In addition to its fixed guns, there aircraft has a tail mount with two 23 mm NR-23 guns. It can fire into the $60-$ arc. It may return fire twice per game turn in response to a gun attacks or conduct a single attack. Roll to hit is 3/2/1 and no modifiers apply except target size. The AtA rating is 4. The ammunition is 6.0.

\item Tail gunner has no ejection seat and can only bail out.

\item RWR from 1960.

\item \href{\detokenize{https://bit.ly/4fQBN9Q}}{ADC page on GitHub}.

\renewcommand{\Fu}{\Fua{\item  Strategic conventional bomber NATO reporting name is Badger-A.

\item DDS capacity is 60 CG and 20 FL or 80 CH.

\item Defensive Guns. Equipped with six 23 mm guns, two in the forward dorsal twin turret, two in the rear ventral twin turret turrets, and two in the tail mount. They can fire in any direction. They may return fire twice per game turn in response to a gun attacks. The roll to hit is 2/1/1 and the AtA rating is 4. Gun attacks are modified only by the target size and possible RE radar ranging. Ammunition is 12.0.

\item Low roll rate (LRR). 

\item Gun Turrets. This variant of the B-26 is equipped with dorsal and ventral turrets each with two .50 cal M2 guns. The turrets can fire in any direction. They may return fire twice per game turn in response to a gun attacks or conduct a single attack. As there is only one gunner, they may fire on only one aircraft per game turn. Roll to hit is 2/1/1 and AtA rating is 2.

\item \href{\detokenize{https://bit.ly/4gPErhi}}{ADC page on GitHub}.

\item Low roll rate (LRR). 

\item Gun Turret. This variant of the B-26 is equipped with a dorsal turret with two .50 cal M2 guns. The turret can fire in any direction at targets that are at the same altitude or higher. It may return fire twice per game turn in response to a gun attacks or conduct a single attack. As there is only one gunner, it may fire on only one aircraft per game turn. Roll to hit is 2/1/1 and AtA rating is 2.

\renewcommand{\Fu}{\Fua{\item  Conventional and nuclear bomber version. A-3B (Early) variant with tail guns. Originally designated A3D-2.

\item High transonic drag (HTD). 

\item Tail Radar. Equipped with a tail radar with an ECCM of 1, arc of 60-, search of 30--10, tracking of 15--10, and lock-on of 7.

\item Defensive Guns. Equipped with a tail turret with two 20 mm M3L guns. They may return fire twice per game turn in response to a gun attacks in the $60-$ arc, but only at a locked-on attacker. No modifiers apply. The roll to hit is 3/2/1 and the AtA rating is 4. Ammunition is 6.0.

\item \href{\detokenize{https://bit.ly/3COXM2p}}{ADC page on GitHub}.

}}
